| 30 | R1 — Reporting dashboard with FIFO valuation, low-stock count, top consumed, COGS (DoD #7) | `666e7c1` | First link in DoD #7's chain. New module `app/dashboard.py` with one route `GET /admin/dashboard` for **Manager + Office** (Admin via the bypass; Workshop + pending 403 — MISSION §3 "Workshop... cannot see aggregated cost data or reports"). Read-only — no mutations, no audit, no movement type, no new tables. **Aggregations** (each is a single round-trip): total inventory value = `SUM(qty_remaining * unit_cost)` across active items' open `cost_layers` rows (joined to `items` filtered `archived_at IS NULL`); low-stock count = `COUNT(items)` where `archived_at IS NULL AND current_qty <= reorder_threshold`; open POs count = `COUNT(purchase_orders)` where `status IN (draft, sent, partially_received)`; overdue checkouts = hardcoded 0 with `<small>` "checkouts not yet implemented" note (C-series will replace it; pinning the test-id `dashboard-overdue-checkouts` now means C-series doesn't have to re-template); top consumed = `SUM(qty)` over `stock_movements WHERE type=OUT AND created_at >= now() - top_days` grouped by `item_id`, joined to `items`, ordered desc, LIMIT 10 (window via `?top_days=N` defaulting 30; clamped `[1, 365]`; non-int / out-of-range silently coerce to default — same posture as M6 pagination); COGS = `SUM(total_cost)` over `stock_movements` where `id IN (SELECT DISTINCT movement_id FROM cost_layer_consumptions) AND created_at BETWEEN cogs_start AND cogs_end+1d` (consumption-row subquery covers OUT + negative-adjustment ADJUSTMENT — both go through `consume_fifo`; adjustment-increase has no consumption row so it's correctly excluded; IN has total_cost set but no consumption row; TRANSFER has neither). The COGS date range is end-inclusive (resolves to `[start 00:00 UTC, end+1 00:00 UTC)`). Default range: last 30 days. Bad-format ISO date 400. **Helpers**: `_coerce_top_days(raw)` (silent coerce on bad / out-of-range), `_parse_cogs_date(raw, *, field_name)` (400 on bad format; blank → None), `_resolve_cogs_range(start, end)` (defaults end=today, start=end-30d). Five aggregation helpers (`_total_inventory_value`, `_low_stock_count`, `_open_pos_count`, `_top_consumed`, `_cogs`) are pure DB reads — no side effects, no Request, no HTTPException. **Decimal coercion**: `func.coalesce(func.sum(...), 0)` returns Decimal under SQLAlchemy's `Numeric(14,4)` round-trip but mypy types `scalar_one()` as Any; defensively branch `if isinstance(total, Decimal): return total else Decimal(str(total))`. The `Decimal(str(...))` lands when SQLite reports SUM as int (all-zero-rows case). Both paths produce a deterministic Decimal output with no precision loss. **Templates / test-ids**: new `dashboard.html` with at-a-glance card row (`dashboard-heading`, `dashboard-total-value`, `dashboard-low-stock-count`, `dashboard-open-pos-count`, `dashboard-overdue-checkouts`); top-consumed table (`dashboard-top-consumed-table` + per-row `dashboard-top-consumed-row` with `data-item-id` + cells `dashboard-top-consumed-sku` / `dashboard-top-consumed-name` / `dashboard-top-consumed-qty` / `dashboard-top-consumed-detail-link`; empty state `dashboard-top-consumed-empty`); two filter forms (`dashboard-top-days-form` + `dashboard-top-days-input` + `dashboard-top-days-submit`; `dashboard-cogs-form` + `dashboard-cogs-start-input` + `dashboard-cogs-end-input` + `dashboard-cogs-submit`); COGS card (`dashboard-cogs-amount`). The `aria-current` is on `path == "/admin/dashboard" or startswith("/admin/dashboard/")` (same tightening pattern as PO2's `nav-reorder` fix). **Tests** (37 new — 32 in `tests/integration/test_dashboard_routes.py` + 5 in `tests/integration/test_layout.py` + 1 e2e walk in `test_dashboard_e2e.py`): `TestDashboardRoleEnforcement` (6) — anon 401; pending 403; Workshop 403; Manager / Office / Admin 200; `TestDashboardTotalValue` (5) — empty zero; single layer `total_value="25.0000"` (10×2.50 column-quantised); multi-item sum (10×2 + 5×3 = 35); archived item's layers excluded; fully-consumed layer contributes 0 (0 + 5×3 = 15); `TestDashboardLowStockCount` (3) — zero state; positive count (2 below + 1 above-threshold = 2); archived items excluded; `TestDashboardOpenPOsCount` (2) — zero; counts draft + sent + partially_received but excludes received + cancelled (3 of 5 in seed); `TestDashboardTopConsumed` (7) — empty when no OUTs; orders by sum(qty) desc with sku-asc tiebreak (B=20 > C=10 > A=5); window excludes 100-day-old OUT (default 30-day); `?top_days=200` includes the 100-day-old OUT; `?top_days=foo` coerces to 30; `?top_days=99999` coerces to 30; TRANSFER not counted; `TestDashboardCOGS` (8) — zero with no movements; sums OUT total_cost (3×2 = "6.0000"); sums ADJUSTMENT decreases AND excludes ADJUSTMENT increases (only the 2-unit decrease counts: 2×2 = "4.0000"); IN movements not counted; default-window picks only recent OUT (6.0000); explicit 90-day window picks up 60-day-old OUT (7×2 = 14); bad `cogs_start` 400; bad `cogs_end` 400; `TestDashboardReadOnly` (1) — GET writes no audit row (compares pre/post audit ids); 5 nav tests in `test_layout.py` — manager / office / admin nav-dashboard visible; The query mirrors PO1's WHERE clause: `Item.archived_at IS NULL AND Item.supplier_id == :sid AND Item.current_qty <= Item.reorder_threshold` ordered by SKU. **Default `qty_ordered` per line**: `item.reorder_qty` when > 0 (manager intent); else the deficit `threshold - current_qty` when > 0 (deficit signal); else `Decimal("1")` (at-threshold-zero-reorder cohort — order at least one to keep the line meaningful, operator can edit later). **Default `expected_unit_cost` per line**: most recent `CostLayer.unit_cost` for the item (`ORDER BY received_at DESC, id DESC`), regardless of `qty_remaining` (a fully-consumed layer is still the most recent unit-cost signal); `None` when no layers exist yet. **Audit shape** — `purchase_order.created`: `entity_type="purchase_order"`, `entity_id=po.id`, `before=None`, `after={supplier_id, status="draft", expected_date=None, notes=None, lines=[{item_id, qty_ordered (str), expected_unit_cost (str|None)}, ...]}`. Decimals stringified with column-quantised scale 4 (e.g. `"50.0000"`) — same wart / convention as M2 / M3 / M4 / M5. **Out of scope (deferred to PO2b)**: edit qty / expected_unit_cost / notes / expected_date on a draft PO; cancel a draft. PO2b will add `POST /admin/purchase-orders/{po_id}` + `purchase_order.updated` audit + the line-level inputs in the detail template. **Schema details**: `purchase_order_lines.po_id` is `ON DELETE CASCADE` (forward-looking parity for a future "destroy a never-sent draft" UX); `qty_received` defaults to `Decimal("0")` with `server_default '0'`; `expected_unit_cost` is nullable; `status` has both Python `default=POStatus.DRAFT` and `server_default='draft'` (belt-and-braces matching `current_qty` / `reorder_threshold` on Items). **No FK on `stock_movements.po_id`** — column is currently always NULL (no PO5 yet); adding the FK is PO5's job. **Templates / test-ids**: detail page — `po-detail-heading` / `po-status-badge` (with `data-status`) / `po-supplier-name` / `po-created-by` / `po-created-at` / `po-expected-date` / `po-notes` / `po-lines-table` / `po-line-row` (with `data-line-id` + `data-item-id`) / `po-line-sku` / `po-line-name` / `po-line-qty-ordered` / `po-line-qty-received` / `po-line-expected-unit-cost` (with `po-line-cost-empty` `<span>` when null) / `po-back-to-list` / `po-back-to-reorder`. List page — `po-list-heading` / `po-status-filter-form` / `po-status-filter` (auto-submitting `<select>`) / `po-list-empty` / `po-list-table` / per-row `po-row` (with `data-po-id`) / `po-row-supplier` / `po-row-status` / `po-row-line-count` / `po-row-created-at` / `po-row-detail-link`. **`nav-reorder` aria-current tightened** from `startswith("/admin/reorder")` to `path == "/admin/reorder" or startswith("/admin/reorder/")` so the future GET endpoints under `/admin/reorder/*` (and the POST target `/admin/reorder/draft-po`) don't accidentally light up the same nav state — pinned by `test_reorder_aria_current_does_not_match_pos_path`. **Tests** (47 new = 38 in new `tests/integration/test_purchase_orders_routes.py` + 6 in `tests/integration/test_layout.py` for `nav-pos` + 3 in `tests/integration/test_reorder_routes.py` for the draft-PO button / blocked-notes; e2e walk extended in-place): role enforcement (10) — anon GET-list / GET-detail / POST-create all 401; pending POST 403; Workshop POST + GET-list + GET-detail all 403; Manager / Office / Admin all 200 GET; POST happy path (7) — single-line PO carries supplier/status/created_by/qty_ordered/qty_received/expected_unit_cost + redirect target; multi-line ordered by SKU (insert C-3/A-1/B-2 → asserted as A-1/B-2/C-3); above-threshold excluded; archived items excluded; other suppliers' items excluded; audit row carries full lines snapshot; flash includes supplier name + line count; default qty_ordered (3) — reorder_qty > 0 → that value; reorder_qty=0 + deficit > 0 → deficit; both zero → fallback 1; default expected_unit_cost (3) — no layers → null; single layer → its unit_cost; multi-layer → newest wins (oldest 2.00 + newest 3.00 → 3.00); GET list (4) — empty state; populated newest-first; `?status_filter=draft` excludes sent; `?status_filter=sent` excludes drafts; GET detail (4) — unknown 404; populated heading + supplier + status badge; lines in SKU order with right cells; null expected_unit_cost shows the empty marker; layout / nav (6) — manager / office / admin nav-pos visible; workshop nav-pos hidden; aria-current on `/admin/purchase-orders`; | 24 | PO1 — Reorder dashboard (items below threshold, grouped by supplier) (DoD #6 partial) | `dc871cb` | First read-only surface in the PO/reorder track. Bucketing happens in Python: rows group by `supplier_id` (or `None` for the "(no supplier)" synthetic bucket), named-supplier groups sort alphabetically (by un-suffixed name so archived suppliers don't slide to the bottom), no-supplier bucket renders last. | 17 | M1 — `cost_layers` + `cost_layer_consumptions` + `stock_movements` + FIFO consumption engine (DoD #5, #6 prerequisite) | `2cd2c6c` | Pure-logic slice — no routes, no UI, no e2e. New `app/cost_engine.py` exposes `record_receipt`, `consume_fifo`, `open_value`, and `InsufficientStockError`. The engine is the **single owner** of `item.current_qty`, `cost_layers.qty_remaining`, and `stock_movements.total_cost` going forward — every M2-M6 / PO5 / ST-series route must call into it rather than mutate those columns directly. New ORM models in `app/models.py`: `StockMovement` (with `MovementType` enum: in/out/adjustment/transfer), `CostLayer` (with `CostLayerSource` enum: po_receipt/manual_in/positive_adjustment), `CostLayerConsumption`. Migration `0010_create_cost_layers_and_movements.py` adds the three tables in dependency order (movements first, then layers, then consumptions — consumptions FK into both layers and movements). **Schema deviation from MISSION §6**: `stock_movements.po_id` and `stock_take_id` are plain `Integer` columns with **no FK constraint** in M1, because `purchase_orders` and `stock_takes` don't exist yet. The FK constraint is a one-line addition in PO2 / ST1's migrations. Documented on the model. **No `archived_at` on any of the three new tables**: they're append-only by mission (§3 "Cost layer history is part of the audit trail and cannot be edited. Corrections are made via new movements"). The engine *does* mutate `cost_layers.qty_remaining` on consumption — that's the one exception, called out in the model docstring (running balance vs frozen received qty). **No DB-level immutability triggers** on the new tables (the audit-log triggers stay scoped to `audit_log` only): the engine is the only writer, and the route layer (M2+) won't expose UPDATE/DELETE paths. If a future "data correction" backdoor is ever added, that's the time to add triggers. **Engine contract**: caller creates the `StockMovement` row, flushes for id, then calls into the engine. Engine takes the movement as input (rather than constructing one) so the route layer owns actor / reason / type / note / po_id wiring. Engine sets `movement.total_cost` as a side effect. Engine raises `ValueError` for input violations (qty <= 0, unit_cost < 0, unflushed movement) and `InsufficientStockError(item_id, requested, available)` for over-consume. **Atomicity** of `consume_fifo`: the available-qty pre-check happens before any mutation, so a raise leaves the DB exactly as it was — verified by `test_over_consumption_is_atomic`. **FIFO order**: `(received_at ASC, id ASC)` — backdated receipts can land ahead of existing layers (e.g. invoice arrives late), and ties broken deterministically by id (verified by `test_ties_broken_by_id_when_received_at_identical` using `freezegun` to force the timestamp tie). The composite `ix_cost_layers_item_received` covers the ORDER BY. **`current_qty` ownership**: chosen "engine owns it" over "route owns it". The alternative invites every M2/M3/M4 route to redo the same arithmetic and risk drift. The engine is the only place that can compute `total_cost` correctly (FIFO sum), so co-locating `current_qty` mutation makes the inventory-level invariant atomic with the cost-level one. The I3 self-critique entry "current_qty not updated when units are created or archived" is now fixable — the M2 route for unique-tracked stock-in will go through the engine and bump `current_qty`. The historical wart (existing unique items show 0 until a movement fires) is still present; a one-shot backfill is M2's call. **No audit-log writes inside the engine**: that's the route's responsibility. The engine is below the audit layer. **No route-level integration in M1**: M2-M6 each add a route that wraps the engine. **Tests**: 44 new (15 in `tests/unit/test_cost_models.py` covering defaults + enum round-trips + FK NOT NULLs + qty_remaining-vs-qty_received independence + plain-Integer po_id/stock_take_id; 29 in `tests/unit/test_cost_engine.py` covering: receipt 9 (correct fields, current_qty increment, total_cost set, received_at default + override, qty/unit_cost validation matrix incl. zero-cost-allowed, unflushed-movement-rejected); single-layer consume 2 (partial + exact); multi-layer consume 3 (FIFO across two layers, exhausted-layer skipped, id-tiebreak with frozen time); errors 6 (over-consume raises with carried-fields, atomic-on-raise, no-layers-at-all, zero qty, negative qty, unflushed movement); isolation 1 (sibling items don't cross-consume); open_value 6 (empty, single, multi-source-sum, exhausted-excluded, partial-included, isolation); combined 2 (full receipt→consume→receipt→consume cycle + positive→negative adjustment cycle). 620 unit+integration (was 576, +44). 9 e2e unchanged. ruff + mypy clean (16 source files; +1 — `app/cost_engine.py`). Migration applies upgrade + downgrade cleanly against a fresh SQLite DB. |
